Head Bento Update\" class=\"resized aligncenter\" style=\"width: 510px; height: 382.019px;\"></a></p>\n<p>Signature first released their Gianni mesh head in <a href=\"https://strawberrysingh.com/2016/10/28/signature-gianni-mesh-head/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">October of 2016</a>, now in <a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/109756825@N06/33926792611\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">April of 2017</a> they have updated this head to bento. This is of course a free update if you previously owned the Gianni mesh head. Here is some information about this head and update:</p>\n<ul>\n<li><strong>Price:</strong> The cost of this bento head is L$3500 and the DEMO is free. The bento update is free so if youâve had this head from before, just hit the redelivery terminal in <a href=\"http://maps.secondlife.com/secondlife/Vadoo%20Reef/108/146/97\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">the mainstore</a> for the update.</li>\n<li><strong>Skin:&nbsp;</strong>It comes with 12 skin tones from Signature and 3 face textures to change the look of the skin: Young, Mature and Gamey.</li>\n<li><strong>Layers:&nbsp;</strong>It comes with 5 layers that you can apply textures to: face, tattoo, eyebrows, beard and hair.</li>\n<li><strong>Omega:&nbsp;</strong><a href=\"http://lovenlustdesigns.blogspot.com/2016/02/signature-gianni.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Signature products are omega-ready</a> so they come with omega pre-installed and donât require a relay HUD.</li>\n<li><strong>Bento:&nbsp;</strong>This head has now been updated and rigged to the bento bones so you are able to adjust it using the Second Life appearance sliders.</li>\n<li><strong>Animations:&nbsp;</strong>It comes with 16 eyes and 16 mouth facial expressions. You can also turn blinking on and off and lips are animated when typing.</li>\n<li><strong>Textures:&nbsp;</strong>It comes with 4 hairbase, 4 beard, 4 brows and 4 eyelash texture options. There are also some extra eyebrows, beards and hairbases available for sale in <a href=\"http://maps.secondlife.com/secondlife/Vadoo%20Reef/108/146/97\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">the mainstore</a> (which I am wearing in this post today).</li>\n<li><strong>Textures Kit:&nbsp;</strong>If you want to make skin appliers for this head, there is a free textures kit available right beside the vendor. The uvmap is the same as the default avatar.</li>\n<li><strong>Customer Service Questions:</strong> If you have any questions about this head, it would be best if you looked at the designersâ profiles, their names are: Mona Delpiaz and Raph Dirval, to see how they&nbsp;prefer to be contacted for customer service issues as I will probably not be able to assist you with that. You can also <a href=\"https://my.secondlife.com/groups/9fb6f687-446a-bdc5-e662-efc1905d6af3\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">join the Signature Mesh Avatar group inworld</a>, the group members are very helpful with questions.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Watch my video on YouTube where I talk about this head:&nbsp;<a href=\"https://youtu.be/gpkaJr6-kYc\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">https://youtu.be/gpkaJr6-kYc</a><br>\n<iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/gpkaJr6-kYc\" width=\"560\" height=\"315\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p>\n<p>Recently Signature mesh body was updated as well, so the hands are also&nbsp;rigged to bento bones, <a href=\"https://strawberrysingh.com/2017/03/27/signature-gianni-mesh-body-bento-hands-update/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">I blogged about that at this link</a>. Now both the body and head are bento enabled.</p>\n<p>Another great thing about Signature is every month they hold a Signature event where all of the items are made specifically for the Signature head or body. <a href=\"https://strawberrysingh.com/2016/12/07/signature-event/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">I have blogged about the Signature event before</a>.
